The Plugin type implements admission.Interface with key methods:\\n   - NewServiceAccount() (line 100): Initializes the admission plugin with MountServiceAccountToken=true by default\\n   - Admit() (line 138): Main admission hook that processes pod creation/update requests\\n   - shouldAutomount() (line 254): Core decision logic that determines whether to mount the token based on: (1) Pod spec's AutomountServiceAccountToken field takes priority, (2) Falls back to ServiceAccount's AutomountServiceAccountToken, (3) Defaults to true for backward compatibility\\n   - mountServiceAccountToken() (line 416): Adds volume and volumeMount definitions to the pod spec for the API token secret, mounting it to /var/run/secrets/kubernetes.io/serviceaccount\\n\\n2. The Plugin type implements admission.Interface with key methods:\\n   - NewServiceAccount() (line 100): Initializes the admission plugin with MountServiceAccountToken=true by default\\n   - Admit() (line 138): Main admission hook that processes pod creation/update requests\\n   - shouldAutomount() (line 254): Core decision logic that determines whether to mount the token based on: (1) Pod spec's AutomountServiceAccountToken field takes priority, (2) Falls back to ServiceAccount's AutomountServiceAccountToken, (3) Defaults to true for backward compatibility\\n   - mountServiceAccountToken() (line 416): Adds volume and volumeMount definitions to the pod spec for the API token secret, mounting it to /var/run/secrets/kubernetes.io/serviceaccount\\n\\n2.
